ncic:VMOCodeSimpleType

simpleType VMOCodeSimpleType in namespace http://release.niem.gov/niem/codes/fbi_ncic/4.2/

Definition

A data type for 2.2: Vehicle Make/Brand (VMA) and Model (VMO) for Automobiles, Light-Duty Vans, Light-Duty Trucks, and Parts
